Allows you to select the desired area on the canvas and place it on different frames than quickly create an animation (for example, changing the position of the object or transparency). You can apply various effects to the selected area: blur, inversion, repaint to another color, and transform the object. It is possible to create your own brushes from the selected area;\r\n* The tool \"Crop\". Allows you to change the size of the canvas to arbitrary by selecting and adjusting the area. There are blanks of the sizes: 1х1, 2х3, 16х9;\r\n* Tool \"Camera\". You can create live photos, Stop motion animation, Timelapse video;\r\n* The tool \"Registrar\". It will help to create animated cards, live painting, captions for animation, movement or scaling of elements in animation.\r\n\r\nPLEASANT THINGS FOR CONVENIENCE\r\n* Undo/Redo/Clear actions. Allows you to speed up the process of drawing - mirror displays the contents;\r\n* Cycle management.  It makes it unnecessary to create additional frames to repeat.
